The following night at Evolve 52, he received a rematch against Thatcher for the Evolve Championship but was defeated.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></p>
<p>Between 22 and 24 January 2016, Galloway and Johnny Gargano entered a three-day tournament to crown the inaugural <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evolve_Tag_Team_Champions" title="Evolve Tag Team Champions">Evolve Tag Team Champions</a>. At Evolve 53, they defeated Catch Point (<a href="/wiki/Drew_Gulak" title="Drew Gulak">Drew Gulak</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TJ_Perkins" title="TJ Perkins">TJ Perkins</a>), at Evolve 54 they defeated <a href="/wiki/The_Bravado_Brothers" title="The Bravado Brothers">The Bravado Brothers</a> and in the finals at Evolve 55, Galloway and Gargano defeated Chris Hero and Tommy End to win the tournament and championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Evolve55_170-0"><a href="#cite_note-Evolve55-170">[170]</a></sup> They lost the title to Drew Gulak and <a href="/wiki/Tracy_Williams" title="Tracy Williams">Tracy Williams</a> on April 2. Following the match Galloway went on a rant claiming he spent his entire title reign as Evolve champion bringing legitimacy to Evolve only for WWE and more specifically NXT to come and squash everything he did while also claiming the companies working relationship with WWE was compromising independent wrestling. Galloway then turned on Gargano, attacking him and Ethan Page.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup> At EVOLVE 60, Galloway defeated Ethan Page. Over the following months, Galloway began aligning himself with other former WWE stars starting with <a href="/wiki/Ethan_Carter_III" title="Ethan Carter III">Ethan Carter III</a> who debuted for the promotion at Evolve 61 attacking Johnny Gargano during his match with Galloway. Continuing the feud, Galloway and EC3 defeated Gargano and TJP in the street fight main-event to Evolve 62 with help from Chris Hero who joined their group and would then claim Cody Rhodes would be joining the group too. The following night at Evolve 63, Galloway defeated Ethan Page in an "Anything Goes" match.</p>
<p>At Evolve 64, a grudge match between Galloway and Drew Gulak was rescheduled as an Evolve Tag Team Championship main-event match between Catch Point and Galloway and the returning <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Taylor_(wrestler)" title="Chuck Taylor (wrestler)">Chuck Taylor</a> (now wrestling under the name "Dustin"). Galloway and DUSTIN were successful in capturing the championships, making Galloway the first ever two-time Evolve Tag Team Champion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Evolve64_172-0"><a href="#cite_note-Evolve64-172">[172]</a></sup> The following night in the main-event of Evolve 65, Galloway defeated Johnny Gargano, following two Future Shock DDT's, a Claymore kick and three Tombstone Piledrivers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup></p>
<p>Dustin and Galloway made their first Evolve Tag Team Championship defense at Evolve 67 on 20 August 2016. They teamed with EC3 against Fred Yehi, TJP and Ethan Page (replacement for Tracy Williams) in a No DQ Six Man Tag where a pin fall on EC3 would result in a title change. At this show, Galloway would also build a feud with his former WWE Tag Team partner Cody Rhodes and veteran announcer <a href="/wiki/Joey_Styles" title="Joey Styles">Joey Styles</a>, after they both refused his invitation to join his "crusade".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup> On November 13, while Galloway was out with an injury, Dustin and Galloway's replacement, Chris Hero, lost the Evolve Tag Team Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup> However, it was later announced that, despite supposed champions Catch Point holding the physical belts, Evolve would continue to recognise both Galloway and Dustin as the Evolve Tag Team Champions.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Independent_circuit_.282014.E2.80.93present.29">Independent circuit (2014–present)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Independent circuit (2014–present)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Following his WWE release, Galloway returned to the Independent circuit. He had some notable successes, even outside of ICW, PWG and Evolve. Wrestling in several different countries, winning titles in Australia, Denmark, Scotland and other regions, while challenging for numerous others.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176"><a href="#cite_note-176">[176]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 30 August 2014, WrestleZone Scotland held their annual "Battle of the Nations" match, which saw Galloway represent Scotland in a winning effort over Andy Wilde, who represented England. The EVOLVE Championship was also contested in this match, with Galloway retaining.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wrestlezonescotland.co.uk_177-0"><a href="#cite_note-wrestlezonescotland.co.uk-177">[177]</a></sup></p>
<p>In November 2014, Galloway debuted for <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Dreamer" title="Tommy Dreamer">Tommy Dreamer</a>'s <a href="/wiki/House_of_Hardcore" title="House of Hardcore">House of Hardcore</a> promotion at "HOH VII", where he was defeated by <a href="/wiki/Austin_Aries" title="Austin Aries">Austin Aries</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 23 January 2015, Galloway competed in a one-night tournament for the International Wrestling Federation (IWF) World Championship. He defeated <a href="/wiki/Tommaso_Ciampa" title="Tommaso Ciampa">Tommaso Ciampa</a> to advance to the finals where he faced <a href="/wiki/Brian_Cage" title="Brian Cage">Brian Cage</a>, Chris Hero and <a href="/wiki/Apollo_Crews" title="Apollo Crews">Uhaa Nation</a> in an elimination four way for the vacant title. Galloway would eliminate Hero by pinfall, but failed to win the title, as he was the last man eliminated following a distraction from Stu Stone which allowed Cage to get the win and the championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 24 April 2015, Galloway defeated Doug Williams to win the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Wrestling_Alliance" title="Scottish Wrestling Alliance">Scottish Wrestling Alliance</a>'s <a href="/wiki/NWA_Scottish_Heavyweight_Championship" title="NWA Scottish Heavyweight Championship">Scottish Heavyweight Championship</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup> He made his first successful defense the following night, defeating SWA Tag Team Champion Mark Coffey in the main event.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181"><a href="#cite_note-181">[181]</a></sup> In a rematch in November 2015, Coffey was successful in defeating Galloway for the title.</p>
<p>In May 2015, Galloway debuted for <a href="/wiki/Asistencia_Asesor%C3%ADa_y_Administraci%C3%B3n" title="Asistencia Asesoría y Administración">AAA</a>, teaming with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Angelico_(wrestler)" title="Angelico (wrestler)">Angelico</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/El_Mesias" title="El Mesias">El Mesias</a> against Matt Hardy, <a href="/wiki/Ken_Anderson_(wrestler)" title="Ken Anderson (wrestler)">Mr. Anderson</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Morrison_(wrestler)" title="John Morrison (wrestler)">Johnny Mundo</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_182-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-182">[182]</a></sup> He returned to Mexico in November to main-event a series of AAA affiliated shows, working three Six Man Tag matches against <a href="/wiki/Rey_Mysterio" title="Rey Mysterio">Rey Mysterio</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue_Demon" title="Blue Demon">Blue Demon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dr._Wagner_Jr." title="Dr. Wagner Jr.">Dr. Wagner Jr.</a>, his partners included <a href="/wiki/Matt_Cross_(wrestler)" title="Matt Cross (wrestler)">Matt Cross</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carlito_(wrestler)" title="Carlito (wrestler)">Carlito</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brodus_Clay" title="Brodus Clay">Brodus</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_182-1"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-182">[182]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183"><a href="#cite_note-183">[183]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184"><a href="#cite_note-184">[184]</a></sup></p>
<p>On August 2015, Galloway debuted for <a href="/wiki/Preston_City_Wrestling" title="Preston City Wrestling">Preston City Wrestling</a>. He began a feud with <a href="/wiki/Noam_Dar" title="Noam Dar">Noam Dar</a>, trading wins and losses, including a surprise appearance at a UK "Supershow" cross-promoted between <a href="/wiki/Ring_of_Honor" title="Ring of Honor">Ring of Honor</a> and PCW.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup> Galloway returned to RPW in October 2015, working two shows. He was defeated in the main-event by <a href="/wiki/Will_Ospreay" title="Will Ospreay">Will Ospreay</a> on the first night and but was then victorious over <a href="/wiki/RPW_Undisputed_British_Tag_Team_Championship" title="RPW Undisputed British Tag Team Championship">RPW Tag Team Champion</a> James Castle on the second.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186"><a href="#cite_note-186">[186]</a></sup> Galloway returned to PCW in February 2016, entering the prestigious "Road to Glory" tournament, successfully defeating Martin Kirby, Mr. Anderson and Noam Dar, before losing to Rampage Brown in the finals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187"><a href="#cite_note-187">[187]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188"><a href="#cite_note-188">[188]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189"><a href="#cite_note-189">[189]</a></sup></p>
<p>In February 2016, it was announced that Galloway would enter the <a href="/wiki/Westside_Xtreme_Wrestling" title="Westside Xtreme Wrestling">Westside Xtreme Wrestling</a> "16 Carat Gold Tournament".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190"><a href="#cite_note-190">[190]</a></sup> Galloway was successful in the first round, defeating <a href="/wiki/Silas_Young" title="Silas Young">Silas Young</a> by pinfall.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191"><a href="#cite_note-191">[191]</a></sup> On night three of the tournament, Galloway defeated <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Angelico_(wrestler)" title="Angelico (wrestler)">Angelico</a> in the quarter-finals before immediately facing <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Axel_Dieter_Jr.&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Axel Dieter Jr. (page does not exist)">Axel Dieter Jr.</a> in the semi-finals, where Galloway was defeated and eliminated from the tournament. wXw announced that Galloway would be returning in September 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192"><a href="#cite_note-192">[192]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 4 June, Galloway became No. 1 Contender for the PCW Heavyweight Championship by winning the "There Can Be Only One" Gauntlet. He defeated Lionheart to qualify and outlasted <a href="/wiki/El_Ligero" title="El Ligero">El Ligero</a>, Dave Mastiff, James Davis, Roy Knight, Zak Knight, Rob Lynch, Alex Boylin, Dave Rayne and Sammy Smooth to win the Gauntlet match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wrestleropesuk.wordpress.com_193-0"><a href="#cite_note-wrestleropesuk.wordpress.com-193">[193]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 25 June, Galloway main-evented the first HD iPPV in European Wrestling history<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup> when he returned to PCW at their "Tribute to the Troops 3" show, where he received his championship opportunity. He was defeated in a PCW Heavyweight Championship triple threat match with <a href="/wiki/Sha_Samuels" title="Sha Samuels">Sha Samuels</a> and Noam Dar, when Dar caused Samuels to submit.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 19 August, Galloway debuted for the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Glory" title="House of Glory">House of Glory</a> promotion in New York, where he faced a surprise opponent of Low Ki in a losing effort, after Low Ki answered Galloway's request for a replacement opponent to the absent Chris Dickinson.</p>
<p>On 26 August, Galloway returned to BCW for the sold-out "Live in Kilmarnock" where he defeated former BCW Tag Team Champion Davey Blaze, before being assaulted post-match by The Aggression (<a href="/wiki/Kid_Fite" title="Kid Fite">Kid Fite</a>, Aaron Echo, Lou King Sharp and Davey Blaze).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196"><a href="#cite_note-196">[196]</a></sup> The following night at Scottish Wrestling Entertainment in Dundee, Galloway was victorious in a No DQ Fatal Four-Way match against <a href="/wiki/Ethan_Carter_III" title="Ethan Carter III">Ethan Carter III</a>, Jack Jester and Joe Hendry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197"><a href="#cite_note-197">[197]</a></sup></p>
<p>Answering Chris Hero's open challenge, Galloway debuted for <a href="/wiki/All_American_Wrestling" title="All American Wrestling">All American Wrestling</a> (AAW) in a losing effort on September 1, 2016 at the "Cero Miedo" event. He returned for "Unstoppable 2016" December 30 to defeat Jeff Cobb and state his intention to wrestle for AAW more frequently.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198"><a href="#cite_note-198">[198]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199"><a href="#cite_note-199">[199]</a></sup> Returning again on January 20, 2017, Galloway was successful in defeating two time <a href="/wiki/AAW_Heavyweight_Championship" title="AAW Heavyweight Championship">AAW Heavyweight Champion</a> Silas Young in Young's AAW farewell match at the "Don't Stop Believing" event.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200"><a href="#cite_note-200">[200]</a></sup></p>
<p>Galloway was badly injured during a WCPW World Championship match with Joseph Conners on 15 September. Galloway was then forced to miss about three months of bookings, including several notable matches, including <a href="/wiki/Damien_Sandow" title="Damien Sandow">Aron Rex</a> for the Impact Grand Championship, Jurn Simmons for the <a href="/wiki/WXw_Unified_World_Wrestling_Championship" title="WXw Unified World Wrestling Championship">WXw Unified World Wrestling Championship</a> as well as dates for EVOLVE, PCW, ICW, NJPW and more. During this time however, Galloway would make non-wrestling appearances for Pro Wrestling Elite, Scottish Wrestling Association and Revolution Pro Wrestling/NJPW.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201"><a href="#cite_note-201">[201]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203"><a href="#cite_note-203">[203]</a></sup></p>
<p>Galloway returned to the ring at ICW's <a href="/wiki/Fear_%26_Loathing_IX" title="Fear &amp; Loathing IX">Fear &amp; Loathing IX</a> event on 20 November as part of Team Black Label in the battle for 100% control of the company.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204"><a href="#cite_note-204">[204]</a></sup> On 26 November for Wrestlecade in North Carolina. He defeated PJ Black.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205"><a href="#cite_note-205">[205]</a></sup></p>
<p>Galloway also made a surprise return for WCPW's "Loaded #16", stating that he would be returning to challenge Joseph Conners for the WCPW World Championship on November 30, 2016, at the "Delete: WCPW" event in a triple threat steel cage match with Conners and Joe Hendry. Galloway was successful in winning the title.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206"><a href="#cite_note-206">[206]</a></sup> The following night, Galloway retained the title against Hendry and Conners in a rematch. On 3 December, Galloway successfully defended the WCPW World Championship against Matt Hardy at BCW's "No Blood, No Sympathy" in Kilmarnock, Scotland.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-207"><a href="#cite_note-207">[207]</a></sup> Galloway again retained the WCPW World Championship at "Lights Out" event, defeating Bully Ray on 13 January 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208"><a href="#cite_note-208">[208]</a></sup> Then on January 21 2017, Galloway defended the WCPW World Championship internationally for the first time, defeating Anthony Bowens at Battle Club Pro's "Fight Forever" show in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Bronx,_New_York_City" title="The Bronx, New York City">The Bronx, New York City</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-209"><a href="#cite_note-209">[209]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Rising_and_various_feuds_.282015.E2.80.932016.29">The Rising and various feuds (2015–2016)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: The Rising and various feuds (2015–2016)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/The_Rising_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Rising (professional wrestling)">The Rising (professional wrestling)</a></div>
<p>On 29 January 2015, Galloway made a surprise debut under his real name for <a href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling</a> during the tapings of <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Impact_Wrestling" title="Impact Wrestling">Impact Wrestling</a></i> as a face in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Glasgow,_Scotland" title="Glasgow, Scotland">Glasgow, Scotland</a>, coming to the aid of <a href="/wiki/TNA_British_Boot_Camp" title="TNA British Boot Camp">TNA British Boot Camp</a> season 2 competitor <a href="/wiki/Grado_(wrestler)" title="Grado (wrestler)">Grado</a> and entering a feud with <a href="/wiki/The_Beat_Down_Clan" title="The Beat Down Clan">The Beat Down Clan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-210"><a href="#cite_note-210">[210]</a></sup> The following night, Galloway competed in his first official match for TNA, answering the Beat Down Clan's challenge, he defeated <a href="/wiki/Kenny_King_(wrestler)" title="Kenny King (wrestler)">Kenny King</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211"><a href="#cite_note-211">[211]</a></sup> On 31 January, Galloway defeated <a href="/wiki/Montel_Vontavious_Porter" title="Montel Vontavious Porter">MVP</a> by disqualification, after the Beat Down Clan interfered in the match. On 27 March <i>Impact Wrestling</i> episode, he formed the stable "<a href="/wiki/The_Rising_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Rising (professional wrestling)">The Rising</a>" with <a href="/wiki/Eli_Drake" title="Eli Drake">Eli Drake</a> and <a href="/wiki/Camacho_(wrestler)" title="Camacho (wrestler)">Micah</a>. On 10 April episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, The Rising defeated The BDC by disqualification when a masked man (<a href="/wiki/Homicide_(wrestler)" title="Homicide (wrestler)">Homicide</a>) ran out and attacked Galloway. On 24 April episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, after a match between Micah and Kenny King ended, Galloway and the members of The Rising came to help only to be beaten down. Afterwards Galloway challenged <a href="/wiki/Low_Ki" title="Low Ki">Low Ki</a> to a Steel Pipe on a Pole match at <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_Justice#2015" title="Hardcore Justice">Hardcore Justice</a>, which Galloway won. At <a href="/wiki/Slammiversary_(2015)" title="Slammiversary (2015)">Slammiversary</a>, Galloway competed at the <a href="/wiki/King_of_the_Mountain_match" title="King of the Mountain match">King of the Mountain match</a> for the vacant <a href="/wiki/TNA_King_of_the_Mountain_Championship" title="TNA King of the Mountain Championship">TNA King of the Mountain Championship</a> in a losing effort. On 1 July episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, The Beat Down Clan defeated The Rising in a 4-on-3 Handicap match, forcing The Rising to dissolve.</p>
<p>On 15 July episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway won a 20-man battle royal to earn the right to face <a href="/wiki/Ethan_Carter_III" title="Ethan Carter III">Ethan Carter III</a> for the <a href="/wiki/TNA_World_Heavyweight_Championship" title="TNA World Heavyweight Championship">TNA World Heavyweight Championship</a> later that night, but he lost the match after his former The Rising teammate, Eli Drake attacked him. At <a href="/wiki/TNA_No_Surrender" title="TNA No Surrender">No Surrender</a>, Galloway was defeated by Drake. A rematch he scheduled at <a href="/wiki/TNA_Turning_Point" title="TNA Turning Point">Turning Point</a> in a No Disqualification match, which Galloway won. On 16 September episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Team TNA (Galloway, <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Lashley" title="Bobby Lashley">Lashley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Davey_Richards" title="Davey Richards">Davey Richards</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Edwards_(wrestler)" title="Eddie Edwards (wrestler)">Eddie Edwards</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bram_(wrestler)" title="Bram (wrestler)">Bram</a>) defeated Team GFW (<a href="/wiki/Jeff_Jarrett" title="Jeff Jarrett">Jeff Jarrett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Young_(wrestler)" title="Eric Young (wrestler)">Eric Young</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chris_Masters" title="Chris Masters">Chris Mordetzky</a>, <a href="/wiki/Curt_Hawkins" title="Curt Hawkins">Brian Myers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sonjay_Dutt" title="Sonjay Dutt">Sonjay Dutt</a>) in a Lethal Lockdown Match to oust GFW from TNA when Galloway pinned Myers after a Future Shock DDT onto a trash can. On 23 September episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, after winning a five-way elimination match against <a href="/wiki/Bram_(wrestler)" title="Bram (wrestler)">Bram</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Lashley" title="Bobby Lashley">Lashley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Davey_Richards" title="Davey Richards">Davey Richards</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Edwards_(wrestler)" title="Eddie Edwards (wrestler)">Eddie Edwards</a>; Galloway became the number one contender for Ethan Carter III's TNA World Heavyweight Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact923_212-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact923-212">[212]</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2015)" title="Bound for Glory (2015)">Bound for Glory</a>, Galloway competed in a three-way match for the world title, which was won by <a href="/wiki/Matt_Hardy" title="Matt Hardy">Matt Hardy</a>. During October and November, Galloway participated in the <a href="/wiki/TNA_World_Title_Series" title="TNA World Title Series">TNA World Title Series</a> for the vacant title, which he qualified to the round of 16 by defeating <a href="/wiki/Bram_(wrestler)" title="Bram (wrestler)">Bram</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rockstar_Spud" title="Rockstar Spud">Rockstar Spud</a> and <a href="/wiki/Grado_(wrestler)" title="Grado (wrestler)">Grado</a>. However, he failed to advance the round of 8 where was defeated in the main event by Lashley, thus being eliminated from the TNA World Title Series.</p>
<p>Galloway then entered a short-lived storyline with <a href="/wiki/Kurt_Angle" title="Kurt Angle">Kurt Angle</a>, at <a href="/wiki/TNA_One_Night_Only#One_Night_Only:_Live" title="TNA One Night Only">TNA One Night Only: Live</a>, Galloway and Angle competed in a 3-Way <a href="/wiki/TNA_World_Tag_Team_Championship" title="TNA World Tag Team Championship">TNA World Tag Team Championship</a> match which was won by <a href="/wiki/The_American_Wolves" title="The American Wolves">The Wolves</a>. On 12 January 2016 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway faced Angle in a losing effort. Galloway would then go on to earn a future TNA World Heavyweight Championship match by grabbing the briefcase that contained said title shot in the 2016 <a href="/wiki/Feast_or_Fired" title="Feast or Fired">Feast or Fired</a> match. Angle and Galloway faced off in a rematch in Manchester, England on 9 February episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, where Galloway was victorious, defeating Angle by submission. After the match he bowed before Angle, showing respect due to it being part of Angle's farewell tour.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213"><a href="#cite_note-213">[213]</a></sup> On the March 1st episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway was defeated by <a href="/wiki/Mike_Bennett_(wrestler)" title="Mike Bennett (wrestler)">Mike Bennett</a>. On the March 15 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway and <a href="/wiki/Gail_Kim" title="Gail Kim">Gail Kim</a> were defeated by Mike Bennett and <a href="/wiki/Maria_Kanellis" title="Maria Kanellis">Maria</a>.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Championship_reigns_and_pursuits_.282016.E2.80.93present.29">Championship reigns and pursuits (2016–present)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Championship reigns and pursuits (2016–present)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 15 March episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway cashed in his <a href="/wiki/Feast_or_Fired" title="Feast or Fired">Feast or Fired</a> briefcase and defeated <a href="/wiki/Matt_Hardy" title="Matt Hardy">Matt Hardy</a> to capture the <a href="/wiki/TNA_World_Heavyweight_Championship" title="TNA World Heavyweight Championship">TNA World Heavyweight Championship</a> for the first time in his career, thus becoming the first-ever Scottish-born TNA World Heavyweight Champion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214"><a href="#cite_note-214">[214]</a></sup> This also would make him the first man to successfully cash-in a Feast or Fired briefcase for the TNA World Heavyweight Championship. Galloway announced his plan to be <i>"the first traveling World Champion since <a href="/wiki/Ric_Flair" title="Ric Flair">Ric Flair</a>"</i> and touted upcoming independent defenses across Europe and the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215"><a href="#cite_note-215">[215]</a></sup> He made his first defense of the title on 29 March episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, defeating <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Hardy" title="Jeff Hardy">Jeff Hardy</a> to retain the title. On 5 April episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway defeated Matt Hardy in a rematch for TNA World Heavyweight Championship. At <a href="/wiki/TNA_Sacrifice#2016" title="TNA Sacrifice">Sacrifice</a>, Galloway would overcome rib injuries inflicted from having been repeatedly speared by <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Lashley" title="Bobby Lashley">Lashley</a> to retain his title over the <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2015)" title="Bound for Glory (2015)">Bound for Gold</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Brodus_Clay" title="Brodus Clay">Tyrus</a>. On 17 May episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway won a lumberjack match against Lashley, who was at the time the #1 contender, by disqualification after he was dragged from the ring and assaulted by the heel lumberjacks, thusly retaining his championship. Galloway would lose the title to Lashley at <a href="/wiki/Slammiversary_(2016)" title="Slammiversary (2016)">Slammiversary</a>, ending his reign at 89 days.</p>
<p>Galloway was twice unsuccessful in regaining his championship from Lashley due to the involvement of Ethan Carter III. Galloway and Carter came to blows in an unsanctioned fight at <a href="/wiki/Destination_X#2016" title="Destination X">Destination X</a> on 12 July which ended in a no contest. Galloway was one of the eight men to enter the <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_Series#2016" title="Bound for Glory Series">Bound for Glory Playoff</a> tournament to challenge for the TNA World Heavyweight Championship at <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2016)" title="Bound for Glory (2016)">Bound for Glory</a>. On 22 July episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway defeated <a href="/wiki/Bram_(wrestler)" title="Bram (wrestler)">Bram</a> in the first round of the tournament but was eliminated from the semi-finals by Mike Bennett following interference from <a href="/wiki/Moose_(wrestler)" title="Moose (wrestler)">Moose</a> and a third inadvertent collision with EC3.</p>
<p>On 25 August episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway faced Ethan Carter III in a losing effort for a world title shot against Lashley at <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2016)" title="Bound for Glory (2016)">Bound for Glory</a>. After the match, he attacked the special guest referee <a href="/wiki/Damien_Sandow" title="Damien Sandow">Aron Rex</a>, turning heel in the process. Galloway and Rex would later feud with each other, with both men joined the qualifying tournament for the inaugural <a href="/wiki/Impact_Grand_Championship" title="Impact Grand Championship">Impact Grand Championship</a>. After defeating <a href="/wiki/Braxton_Sutter" title="Braxton Sutter">Braxton Sutter</a> in the quarterfinals and <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Edwards_(wrestler)" title="Eddie Edwards (wrestler)">Eddie Edwards</a> (via split decision) in the semifinals, he was scheduled to face Rex in the finals at Bound for Glory to crown the first Grand Champion, but due to an injury he was replaced by Edwards. On 8 December episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Galloway made his return by interrupting the Impact Grand Champion <a href="/wiki/Moose_(wrestler)" title="Moose (wrestler)">Moose</a> and criticizing the company. On 19 January 2017, Galloway made his in-ring return to TNA, defeating Moose to win the Impact Grand Championship. Galloway would retain the title three times, defeating Moose, Rob Ryzin and Mahabali Shera<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216"><a href="#cite_note-216">[216]</a></sup> before losing the championship back to Moose via split decision in a second rematch.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-411mania.com_217-0"><a href="#cite_note-411mania.com-217">[217]</a></sup> At this time, Galloway's TNA status is unknown.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218"><a href="#cite_note-218">[218]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pro_Wrestling_Guerrilla_.282015.E2.80.93present.29">Pro Wrestling Guerrilla (2015–present)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Pro Wrestling Guerrilla (2015–present)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Galloway debuted for <a href="/wiki/Pro_Wrestling_Guerrilla" title="Pro Wrestling Guerrilla">Pro Wrestling Guerrilla</a> in August 2015, competing in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Los_Angeles_(professional_wrestling)" title="Battle of Los Angeles (professional wrestling)">Battle of Los Angeles</a> tournament. He was eliminated by eventual finalist "Speedball" <a href="/wiki/Mike_Bailey_(wrestler)" title="Mike Bailey (wrestler)">Mike Bailey</a> on Night 2 before teaming with <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Taylor_(wrestler)" title="Chuck Taylor (wrestler)">Chuck Taylor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aero_Star" title="Aero Star">Aero Star</a>, <a href="/wiki/Drew_Gulak" title="Drew Gulak">Drew Gulak</a> and Trent in a winning ten man tag effort the following night, against Timothy Thatcher, <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Everett" title="Andrew Everett">Andrew Everett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Drago_(wrestler)" title="Drago (wrestler)">Drago</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mark_Andrews_(wrestler)" title="Mark Andrews (wrestler)">Mark Andrews</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tommaso_Ciampa" title="Tommaso Ciampa">Tommaso Ciampa</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219"><a href="#cite_note-219">[219]</a></sup></p>
<p>Galloway returned to PWG on 2 Jan 2016 for "Lemmy", where he scored his first PWG singles victory over former <a href="/wiki/PWG_World_Tag_Team_Championship" title="PWG World Tag Team Championship">PWG World Tag Team Champion</a> <a href="/wiki/Jack_Evans_(wrestler)" title="Jack Evans (wrestler)">Jack Evans</a>. Galloway was granted a title shot at "Bowie" on 12 Feb 2016, challenging former rival Roderick Strong for the <a href="/wiki/PWG_World_Championship" title="PWG World Championship">PWG World Championship</a> but was unsuccessful.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220"><a href="#cite_note-220">[220]</a></sup> Following the match, Galloway was attacked by both Strong and <a href="/wiki/Adam_Cole" title="Adam Cole">Adam Cole</a> until <a href="/wiki/Zack_Sabre_Jr." title="Zack Sabre Jr.">Zack Sabre Jr.</a> made the save.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221"><a href="#cite_note-221">[221]</a></sup> Galloway would return to PWG in March to face Trent and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trevor_Lee_(wrestler)" title="Trevor Lee (wrestler)">Trevor Lee</a> at "All Star Weekend 12", despite controlling most of the offense in these matches, Galloway lost both contests.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222"><a href="#cite_note-222">[222]</a></sup></p>
<p>Galloway returned to winning ways in PWG at "Prince" on 20 May 2016, issuing an open challenge and defeating <a href="/wiki/Michael_Elgin" title="Michael Elgin">Michael Elgin</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223"><a href="#cite_note-223">[223]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Drew_Galloway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Having grown up in <a href="/wiki/Prestwick" title="Prestwick">Prestwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ayrshire" title="Ayrshire">Ayrshire</a>, Galloway studied at <a href="/wiki/Prestwick_Academy" title="Prestwick Academy">Prestwick Academy</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224"><a href="#cite_note-224">[224]</a></sup> and completed a <a href="/wiki/Criminology" title="Criminology">criminology</a> degree at <a href="/wiki/Glasgow_Caledonian_University" title="Glasgow Caledonian University">Glasgow Caledonian University</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rangers_225-0"><a href="#cite_note-rangers-225">[225]</a></sup> He is a supporter of Scottish <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> team <a href="/wiki/Rangers_F.C." title="Rangers F.C.">Rangers</a> and considered being a professional football player when he was younger. He played for many seasons at Prestwick Boys club, normally in defence before concentrating his sporting activities on wrestling.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-newco_226-0"><a href="#cite_note-newco-226">[226]</a></sup></p>
<p>In July 2009, Galloway proposed to <a href="/wiki/Taryn_Terrell" title="Taryn Terrell">Taryn Terrell</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-towed_227-0"><a href="#cite_note-towed-227">[227]</a></sup> and reports of their intention to wed surfaced in January 2010 in the <a href="/wiki/Dave_Meltzer#Wrestling_Observer_Newsletter" title="Dave Meltzer">Wrestling Observer Newsletter</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228"><a href="#cite_note-228">[228]</a></sup> The couple married in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Las_Vegas,_Nevada" title="Las Vegas, Nevada">Las Vegas</a> in May 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-license_229-0"><a href="#cite_note-license-229">[229]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230"><a href="#cite_note-230">[230]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Caldwell_231-0"><a href="#cite_note-Caldwell-231">[231]</a></sup> On 24 May 2011, Terrell announced that she and Galloway were divorcing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Caldwell_231-1"><a href="#cite_note-Caldwell-231">[231]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 3 November 2012, Galloway's mother, Angela, died at the age of 51.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-232"><a href="#cite_note-232">[232]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 17 February 2016, Galloway got engaged in Las Vegas.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233"><a href="#cite_note-233">[233]</a></sup> On 9 December, he married his long-term partner Kaitlyn Frohnapfel in St. Petersburg, Fl.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-234"><a href="#cite_note-234">[234]</a></sup></p>
